                    <li class="nav-item"><a class="nav-link js-scroll-trigger" href="index.html#Work">Work</a></li>
                    <li class="nav-item"><a class="nav-link js-scroll-trigger" href="contact.html">Contact</a></li>
                </ul>
            </div>
        </div>
    </nav>
</
```
